SimpleDate [ScnCommunityUtils]
Simple Date 0.X
This page is giving short introduction to the component with summary of the change status (green/yellow/red)

Date-based navigation (roll days, months) in BIAL script directly, format days to own formats.

Link to blog: Design Studio SDK: Simple Date Object Component

This page is listing community blogs on this component, follow this link to learn more.
This page is listing all changes which have been done on this component with corresponding test status (green: ok, red: not ok, yellow: untested), follow this link to learn more.
This page is listing all example applications with this component, follow this link to learn more.
This page will bring more "about" details (generated)

FUNCTIONS IN DETAIL

String
format		 Method for custom format by string pattern, supports:
YYYY: year
YY: 2-digit year
MM: 2-digit
M: month
DD: 2-digit day
D: day
WW: 2-digit calendar week
W: calendar week
Q: quarter

NameTypeHelp
formatPattern String
Source Code var resultString = formatPattern;
    resultString = resultString.replace("YYYY", this.getYear());
    resultString = resultString.replace("YY", this.getYear() % 100);
    
    if(this.getMonth() < 10) {
      resultString = resultString.replace("MM", "0" + this.getMonth());  
      resultString = resultString.replace("M", this.getMonth());
    } else {
      resultString = resultString.replace("MM", this.getMonth());
    }
    
    if(this.getDay() < 10) {
      resultString = resultString.replace("DD", "0" + this.getDay());
      resultString = resultString.replace("D", this.getDay());
    } else {
      resultString = resultString.replace("DD", this.getDay());
    }
    
    if(this.getCalendarWeek() < 10) {
      resultString = resultString.replace("WW", "0" + this.getCalendarWeek());
      resultString = resultString.replace("W", this.getCalendarWeek());
    } else {
      resultString = resultString.replace("WW", this.getCalendarWeek());
    }
    
    resultString = resultString.replace("Q", this.getQuarter());

    return resultString;

1 is January, 12 is December

    return dayJson.m;
 
int
getQuarter		 Simple getter for Quarter of current date
Months 1-3 are Quarter 1, Months 4-6 are Quarter 2, Months 7-9 are Quarter 3, Months 10-12 are Quarter 4
Source Code var dayJson = JSON.parse(this.oneDay);
  
    var quarter = Math.ceil(dayJson.m / 3);
  
     return quarter;

void
initializeWithDate		 Initialization method with year, month and day

NameTypeHelp
year int Year
month int Month (1 for January up to 12 for December)
day int Day
Source Code var monthString = "" + month;
    if(month < 10) {
      monthString = "0" + monthString;
    }
    
    var dayString = "" + day;
    if(day < 10) {
      dayString = "0" + dayString;
    }

    var internalDate = "" + year + monthString + dayString;
    
    this.initializeWithInternalDate(internalDate);
 
void
initializeWithInternalDate		 Initialization method with internal date format (YYYYMMDD)
You can use the APPLICATION.getInfo().dateNowInternalFormat to get the current date

NameTypeHelp
internalDate String Date in internal format YYYYMMDD eg. 20140812
Source Code this.internal_setup();
  
    var daysJson = JSON.parse(this.days);
  
    var lOneDay = {};
  
    for (var i = 0; i < daysJson.length; i++) {
      var k = daysJson[i].k;
      
      if(k == internalDate) {
        lOneDay = daysJson[i];
        break;
      }
    }
    
    this.oneDay = JSON.stringify(lOneDay);
    this.days = "";

void
internal_rollMonths		 Internal Method, do not use in Scripts

NameTypeHelp
months int
Source Code var index = this.internal_getIndex();
  
    var daysJson = JSON.parse(this.days);
    
    var lOneDay;
    
    var arrayIndex = index - daysJson[0].i;
  
    var beforeYear = getYear();
    var beforeMonth = getMonth();
    var beforeDay = getDay();
  
    var monthBeforeEnteringLoop = beforeMonth;
      
    if(months < 0) {
      // index must go up
      
      for (var i = arrayIndex + 1; i < daysJson.length; i++) {
        
        var year = daysJson[i].y;
        var month = daysJson[i].m;
        var day = daysJson[i].d;
        
        // we check how many months we already have processed
        if(month != monthBeforeEnteringLoop) {
          monthBeforeEnteringLoop = month;
          months = months + 1;
        }
        
        if(months == 0) {
          // already in the targeted month, now we search for the day
          
          if(day == beforeDay || day < beforeDay) {
            lOneDay = daysJson[i];
            break;
          }
        }
      }
      
      if(lOneDay == undefined) {
        lOneDay = daysJson[daysJson.length - 1];    
      }
    } else {
      // index must go down
  
      for (var i = arrayIndex - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        
        var year = daysJson[i].y;
        var month = daysJson[i].m;
        var day = daysJson[i].d;
        
        // we check how many months we already have processed
        if(month != monthBeforeEnteringLoop) {
          monthBeforeEnteringLoop = month;
          months = months - 1;
        }
        
        if(months == 0) {
          // already in the targeted month, now we search for the day
          
          lOneDay = daysJson[i];
          
          if(day == beforeDay) {
            break;
          }
        }

        // emergency exit in case this month has lower numbers of days
        if(months < 0 && lOneDay != undefined) {
          break;
        }
      }
      
      if(lOneDay == undefined) {
        lOneDay = daysJson[0];
      }
    }
  
    this.oneDay = JSON.stringify(lOneDay);
 
void
internal_setDateByIndex		 Internal Method, do not use in Scripts

NameTypeHelp
index int
Source Code this.internal_setup();
    var daysJson = JSON.parse(this.days);
  
    var lOneDay;
    
    if(index > daysJson.lenght - 1) {
      lOneDay = daysJson[daysJson.lenght - 1];  
    } else if(index < 0) {
      lOneDay = daysJson[0];
    } else {
      lOneDay = daysJson[index - daysJson[0].i];    
    }

    this.oneDay = JSON.stringify(lOneDay);

String
internal_toString		 Internal Method, do not use in Scripts
Source Code return "Day of Year: " + this.getDayOfYear() + "\n"
     + "Day of Month: " + this.getDay() + "\n\n"
     + "Day of Week: " + this.getDayOfWeek() + "\n"
     + "Calendar Week: " + this.getCalendarWeek() + "\n"
     + "Month: " + this.getMonth() + "\n"
     + "Quarter: " + this.getQuarter() + "\n"
     + "Year: " + this.getYear() + "\n"
     // + "Day Name: " + this.getDayName() + "\n"
     // + "Month Name: " + this.getMonthName() + "\n"
     + "Formatted: " + this.getDay() + "." + this.getMonth() + "." + this.getYear() + "\n"
     + "Formatted [DD.MM.YYYY WW]: " + this.format("DD.MM.YYYY WW") + "\n"
     + "Formatted [MM/DD/YYYY WW]: " + this.format("MM/DD/YYYY WW") + "\n\n"
     + "";
 
void
rollDays		 Roll days up and down, negative numbers are rolling down

NameTypeHelp
days int Days to Roll
Source Code var index = this.internal_getIndex();
  
    index = index - days;
    
    internal_setDateByIndex(index);
    this.days = "";
 
void
rollMonths		 Roll months up and down, negative numbers are rolling down.
This roll is keeping the day, as far it is possible. If the target month does not have this day, it will take the last day. Eg. 31. March 2014 -> rollMonth(-1) will lead to 28. February 2014.
Same effect as rollDays(weeks 7);

NameTypeHelp
months int Months to Roll
Source Code this.internal_setup();

    internal_rollMonths(months);
    
    this.days = "";
 
void
rollWeeks		 Roll days up and down, negative numbers are rolling down.
Same effect as rollDays(weeks 7);

NameTypeHelp
weeks int Weeks to Roll
Source Code var index = this.internal_getIndex();
  
    index = index - (weeks * 7);
    
    internal_setDateByIndex(index);
    this.days = "";
 
void
rollYears		 Roll years up and down, negative numbers are rolling down.
This roll is keeping the day, as far it is possible. If the target month does not have this day, it will take the last day. Eg. 29. March 2012 -> rollYear(-1) will lead to 28. February 2011.
Same effect as rollMonths(years 12);

NameTypeHelp
years int Years to Roll
Source Code this.internal_setup();

    internal_rollMonths(years * 12);
    
    this.days = "";
 
String
toLocaleString		 Returns currently only internal format as locale handling is not available yet
Source Code return format("YYYYMMDD");
